ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM C
[See Rule 7]
FORM OF NOTICE UNDER SUB-SECTION(1) OF SECTION 3 OF THE TAMIL NADU ACQUISITION OF LANDS 
FOR INDUSTRIAL PURPOSES ACT, 1997 
(CLA-SIP/2024/34/01/02/0001)
No.VI(1)/ 709(b-1)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been 
decided that the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or 
managed by the Managing Director, SIPCOT. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 17.7800 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit,Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

Total extent to be acquired : 19.7150 (Hectares) 
(CLA-SIP/2024/34/11/02/0001)
No.VI(1)/709(b-3)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be acquired 
for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 23.6250 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvannamalai and Special Tahsildar(LA), 
Unit ,Tiruvannamalai may be inspected on any day during office hours.
Tඐඍ Sඋඐඍඌඝඔඍ
Tiruvannamalai District, Cheyyar Taluk, Elaneerkundram Village
(Unit No : 11, Block No : 02)

NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 13.9550 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - Cheyyar Industrial Park Phase III.

Unit, Tiruvannamalai which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisfied that the lands specified in the schedule below to be 
acquired for industrial purpose to wit to SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park and it having already been decided that 
the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands specified in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.1200 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.
The plan of the lands are kept in the office of the Special DRO(LA), Tiruvallur and Special Tahsildar (LA), 
Unit, Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during office hours.

the amount of compensation to be awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by 
the Managing Director, SIPCOT, Chennai. The following notice is issued under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the 
Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997. (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999)
NOTICE
Under sub-section(1) of section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Lands for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands speciﬁ ed in the Schedule below 
measuring an extent of 11.2700 hectares to the same, a little more or less needed for industrial purpose wit, for 
SIPCOT - SIPCOT Industrial Park.

Unit, Tiruvallur which may be inspected on any day during oﬃ  ce hours.

(LAI-1/8586020/2024)
No.VI(1)/709(b-10)/2024.
The Government of Tamil Nadu having been satisﬁed that the lands speciﬁed in the Schedule below to be 
acquired for Industrial Purposes to wit for the Formation of New Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Morappur and 
Dharmapuri in Morappur, Rasalampatti, Kurumpatti, Kondayampatty, Chennampatti and Veppachennampatti Villages 
of Harur Taluk in Dharmapuri District, and it having already been decided that the amount of compensation to be 
awarded for the lands are to be paid out of the funds controlled or managed by Southern Railways. The following 
notice is issued under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 
1997 (Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999).
NOTICE
Under sub-section (1) of Section 3 of the Tamil Nadu Acquisition of Land for Industrial Purposes Act, 1997 
(Tamil Nadu Act 10 of 1999), the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby acquires the lands speciﬁed in the Schedule below 
measuring 75109 Sq.mtrs., to the same, a little more or less needed for Industrial Purposes to wit for the Formation 
of New Broad-Gauge Railway Line between Morappur and Dharmapuri in Morappur, Rasalampatti, Kurumpatti, 
Kondayampatty, Chennampatti and Veppachennampatti Villages of Harur Taluk in Dharmapuri District.
The plan of the lands is kept in the oﬃce of the Land Acquisition Oﬃcer, District Revenue Oﬃcer and Special 
Tahsildar (LA), Dharmapuri which may be inspected on any day during oﬃ  ce hours.
